\hypertarget{asyncfatfs_8c_ad97fdbe2e2d521aa61195186031a4111}{\index{asyncfatfs.\+c@{asyncfatfs.\+c}!O\+N\+L\+Y\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+S\+E\+\_\+\+F\+O\+R\+\_\+\+T\+E\+S\+T\+I\+N\+G@{O\+N\+L\+Y\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+S\+E\+\_\+\+F\+O\+R\+\_\+\+T\+E\+S\+T\+I\+N\+G}}
\index{O\+N\+L\+Y\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+S\+E\+\_\+\+F\+O\+R\+\_\+\+T\+E\+S\+T\+I\+N\+G@{O\+N\+L\+Y\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+S\+E\+\_\+\+F\+O\+R\+\_\+\+T\+E\+S\+T\+I\+N\+G}!asyncfatfs.\+c@{asyncfatfs.\+c}}
\subsubsection[{O\+N\+L\+Y\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+S\+E\+\_\+\+F\+O\+R\+\_\+\+T\+E\+S\+T\+I\+N\+G}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}\#define O\+N\+L\+Y\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+S\+E\+\_\+\+F\+O\+R\+\_\+\+T\+E\+S\+T\+I\+N\+G~static}}\label{asyncfatfs_8c_ad97fdbe2e2d521aa61195186031a4111}
This is a F\+A\+T16/\+F\+A\+T32 filesystem for S\+D cards which uses asynchronous operations\+: The caller need never wait for the S\+D card to be ready.

On top of the regular F\+A\+T32 concepts, we add the idea of a \char`\"{}super cluster\char`\"{}. Given one F\+A\+T sector, a super cluster is the series of clusters which corresponds to all of the cluster entries in that F\+A\+T sector. If files are allocated on super-\/cluster boundaries, they will have F\+A\+T sectors which are dedicated to them and independent of all other files.

We can pre-\/allocate a \char`\"{}freefile\char`\"{} which is a file on disk made up of contiguous superclusters. Then when we want to allocate a file on disk, we can carve it out of the freefile, and know that the clusters will be contiguous without needing to read the F\+A\+T at all (the freefile's F\+A\+T is completely determined from its start cluster and file size, which we get from the directory entry). This allows for extremely fast append-\/only logging.

\subsection{Function Documentation}
\hypertarget{asyncfatfs_8c_a4d6c3c1e8650e95969df18cd9bbf4dbf}{\index{asyncfatfs.\+c@{asyncfatfs.\+c}!afatfs\+\_\+chdir@{afatfs\+\_\+chdir}}
\index{afatfs\+\_\+chdir@{afatfs\+\_\+chdir}!asyncfatfs.\+c@{asyncfatfs.\+c}}
\subsubsection[{afatfs\+\_\+chdir}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}bool afatfs\+\_\+chdir (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf afatfs\+File\+Ptr\+\_\+t}}]{directory}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{asyncfatfs_8c_a4d6c3c1e8650e95969df18cd9bbf4dbf}
Change the working directory to the directory with the given handle (use fopen). Pass N\+U\+L\+L for {\ttfamily directory} in order to change to the root directory.

Returns true on success, false if you should call again later to retry. After changing into a directory, your handle to that directory may be closed by fclose(). 

Here is the call graph for this function\+:\nopagebreak

\begin{center}

\includegraphics[width=256pt]{asyncfatfs_8c_a4d6c3c1e8650e95969df18cd9bbf4dbf_cgraph}

\hypertarget{asyncfatfs_8c_a60f4c0414d58f4f5c9a0bb20d61469d9}{\index{asyncfatfs.\+c@{asyncfatfs.\+c}!afatfs\+\_\+fclose@{afatfs\+\_\+fclose}}

\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{asyncfatfs_8c_a60f4c0414d58f4f5c9a0bb20d61469d9}
Returns true if an operation was successfully queued to close the file and destroy the file handle. If the file is currently busy, false is returned and you should retry later.

If provided, the callback will be called after the operation completes (pass N\+U\+L\+L for no callback).

If this function returns true, you should not make any further calls to the file (as the handle might be reused for a new file). \hypertarget{asyncfatfs_8c_a01b0181c718d610e239774381712b136}{\index{asyncfatfs.\+c@{asyncfatfs.\+c}!afatfs\+\_\+feof@{afatfs\+\_\+feof}}

\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{asyncfatfs_8c_a01b0181c718d610e239774381712b136}

Release resources associated with a find operation. Calling this more than once is harmless. \hypertarget{asyncfatfs_8c_ab482a4ea39b08a1b875a775d5864a096}{\index{asyncfatfs.\+c@{asyncfatfs.\+c}!afatfs\+\_\+find\+Next@{afatfs\+\_\+find\+Next}}

Attempt to advance the directory pointer {\ttfamily finder} to the next entry in the directory.

Returns\+: A\+F\+A\+T\+F\+S\+\_\+\+O\+P\+E\+R\+A\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+S\+U\+C\+C\+E\+S\+S -\/ A pointer to the next directory entry has been loaded into $\ast$dir\+Entry. If the directory was exhausted then $\ast$dir\+Entry will be set to N\+U\+L\+L. A\+F\+A\+T\+F\+S\+\_\+\+O\+P\+E\+R\+A\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+I\+N\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+G\+R\+E\+S\+S -\/ The disk is busy. The pointer is not advanced, call again later to retry. \hypertarget{asyncfatfs_8c_a8d8a9af02b4c68cdd5e1581a1573b36c}{\index{asyncfatfs.\+c@{asyncfatfs.\+c}!afatfs\+\_\+flush@{afatfs\+\_\+flush}}

\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{asyncfatfs_8c_a8d8a9af02b4c68cdd5e1581a1573b36c}
Attempt to flush dirty cache pages out to the sdcard, returning true if all flushable data has been flushed. \hypertarget{asyncfatfs_8c_a591cb34261282fc66547cc90c5a2146e}{\index{asyncfatfs.\+c@{asyncfatfs.\+c}!afatfs\+\_\+fopen@{afatfs\+\_\+fopen}}
\index{afatfs\+\_\+fopen@{afatfs\+\_\+fopen}!asyncfatfs.\+c@{asyncfatfs.\+c}}
\subsubsection[{afatfs\+\_\+fopen}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}bool afatfs\+\_\+fopen (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{const char $\ast$}]{filename, }
\item[{const char $\ast$}]{mode, }
\item[{{\bf afatfs\+File\+Callback\+\_\+t}}]{complete}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{asyncfatfs_8c_a591cb34261282fc66547cc90c5a2146e}
Begin the process of opening a file with the given name in the current working directory (paths in the filename are not supported) using the given mode.

To open the current working directory, pass \char`\"{}.\char`\"{} for filename.

The complete() callback is called when finished with either a file handle (file was opened) or N\+U\+L\+L upon failure.

Supported file mode strings\+:

r -\/ Read from an existing file w -\/ Create a file for write access, if the file already exists then truncate it a -\/ Create a file for write access to the end of the file only, if the file already exists then append to it

r+ -\/ Read and write from an existing file w+ -\/ Read and write from an existing file, if the file doesn't already exist it is created a+ -\/ Read from or append to an existing file, if the file doesn't already exist it is created T\+O\+D\+O

as -\/ Create a new file which is stored contiguously on disk (high performance mode/freefile) for append or write ws If the file is already non-\/empty or freefile support is not compiled in then it will fall back to non-\/contiguous operation.

All other mode strings are illegal. In particular, don't add \char`\"{}b\char`\"{} to the end of the mode string.

Returns false if the the open failed really early (out of file handles). \hypertarget{asyncfatfs_8c_a48cc60f56884206251a165dd3a372f09}{\index{asyncfatfs.\+c@{asyncfatfs.\+c}!afatfs\+\_\+fputc@{afatfs\+\_\+fputc}}
\index{afatfs\+\_\+fputc@{afatfs\+\_\+fputc}!asyncfatfs.\+c@{asyncfatfs.\+c}}

\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf afatfs\+File\+Ptr\+\_\+t}}]{file, }
\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{c}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{asyncfatfs_8c_a48cc60f56884206251a165dd3a372f09}
Write a single character to the file at the current cursor position. If the cache is too busy to accept the write, it is silently dropped.

Attempt to read {\ttfamily len} bytes from {\ttfamily file} into the {\ttfamily buffer}.

Returns the number of bytes actually read.

0 will be returned when\+: The filesystem is busy (try again later) E\+O\+F was reached (check afatfs\+\_\+is\+Eof())

Fewer bytes than requested will be read when\+: The read spans a A\+F\+A\+T\+F\+S\+\_\+\+S\+E\+C\+T\+O\+R\+\_\+\+S\+I\+Z\+E boundary and the following sector was not available in the cache yet. \hypertarget{asyncfatfs_8c_a15689d94e5c0267c44229c608342f2df}{\index{asyncfatfs.\+c@{asyncfatfs.\+c}!afatfs\+\_\+fseek@{afatfs\+\_\+fseek}}
\index{afatfs\+\_\+fseek@{afatfs\+\_\+fseek}!asyncfatfs.\+c@{asyncfatfs.\+c}}

\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf afatfs\+File\+Ptr\+\_\+t}}]{file, }
\item[{int32\+\_\+t}]{offset, }
\item[{{\bf afatfs\+Seek\+\_\+e}}]{whence}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{asyncfatfs_8c_a15689d94e5c0267c44229c608342f2df}
Attempt to seek the file cursor from the given point ({\ttfamily whence}) by the given offset, just like C's fseek().

A\+F\+A\+T\+F\+S\+\_\+\+S\+E\+E\+K\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T with offset 0 will always return A\+F\+A\+T\+F\+S\+\_\+\+O\+P\+E\+R\+A\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+S\+U\+C\+C\+E\+S\+S.

Returns\+: A\+F\+A\+T\+F\+S\+\_\+\+O\+P\+E\+R\+A\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+S\+U\+C\+C\+E\+S\+S -\/ The seek was completed immediately A\+F\+A\+T\+F\+S\+\_\+\+O\+P\+E\+R\+A\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+I\+N\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+G\+R\+E\+S\+S -\/ The seek was queued and will complete later. Feel free to attempt read/write operations on the file, they'll fail until the seek is complete. A\+F\+A\+T\+F\+S\+\_\+\+O\+P\+E\+R\+A\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+F\+A\+I\+L\+U\+R\+E -\/ The seek could not be queued because the file was busy with another operation, try again later. \hypertarget{asyncfatfs_8c_aa9edffdb315d8ab73067b25be34d105b}{\index{asyncfatfs.\+c@{asyncfatfs.\+c}!afatfs\+\_\+ftell@{afatfs\+\_\+ftell}}
